# Content Package 1: The beauty salon that found five unread visitor questions on Tuesday — and no way to reach any of them

## 1. PACKAGE OVERVIEW

- **package id:** `ba3d2e09-1023-4f74-9575-7007c8ed07c0`
- **title:** The beauty salon that found five unread visitor questions on Tuesday — and no way to reach any of them
- **strategy item:** `a471f235-fed8-4c9b-ad4f-b3a885115b8e` — topic: The beauty salon that found five unread visitor questions on Tuesday — and no way to reach any of them
- **angle (strategy):** A salon owner opens her website analytics on a Tuesday morning and sees that five people browsed her services page over the weekend, spent time on the booking section, and left without filling out a single form. No names, no emails, no phone numbers — just sessions that ended in silence. The hook dramatizes the specific moment she realizes those weren't just bounces; they were real people ready to book, who had a question she was never there to answer. The content walks through why a static website with a contact form is not the same as being available, and why visitors with an unanswered question almost never come back.
- **funnel stage:** problem_aware
- **goal:** lead_generation _(projekt; v package_brief není uloženo)_
- **CTA:** Create your AI assistant — let your website answer while the salon is closed. (type: sign_up)
- **language:** en
- **visual profile (job/brief):** NATURAL
- **resolved visual profile (project):** MINIMAL (source: auto)
- **voice:** shimmer
- **voice instructions:**

Speak naturally for a short vertical social video. Language: en. Tone: Simple and accessible; Direct and action-oriented; Transparent and honest; Friendly and approachable; Concise and practical. Read the script exactly; do not add or skip words. Delivery: direct, empathetic, slightly frustrated. Delivery: thoughtful, reflective, steady pacing. Delivery: confident, concise, not aggressive. Opening: alert, clipped first phrase — not shouted. Then settle into conversational body delivery. Use spok


- **semantic motion enabled:** ano (default)
- **scene history decisions:**

```json
[]
```

- **presentation analyzer summary (decisions count):** 5
- **allowed_scene_types:** ["IMAGE","CHECKLIST","QUOTE","PHONE","CTA"]
- **creative_mode:** observation
- **hook:** Urgent question dies in silence.

## 2. COMPLETE VOICEOVER

Urgent question dies in silence. She typed it Saturday night — which color treatment, how long, can I book tomorrow. Your site said nothing. No chat. No answer. Just a contact form that felt like a locked door. By Tuesday morning you had five sessions, zero leads. Those weren't bounces. They were ready. A static website isn't the same as being available. Your next visitor deserves an answer — even when you're not there.

[
  {
    "id": "scene-1",

      "media": {
        "source": "ai",
        "image_prompt": "Soft polished 3D render, portrait 9:16 vertical frame, urban gray-blue ambient palette, overcast diffused daylight, quiet optimism mood, symmetrical calm composition, slightly above table height camera angle, implied human presence just off-screen. ## 10. FINAL REVIEW

Technické hodnocení (na základě uložených rozhodnutí generátoru a analyzáru, ne marketing).

### Proč AI zvolila scene types

- Model vygeneroval výhradně **IMAGE** scény v `visual_scenes` / `scenes`. Analyzer u každé scény zaznamenal rule `allowed`, reason `image scene` — typ se nezměnil.
- `prompt_presentation_types` v briefu: ["IMAGE","CHECKLIST","PHONE","QUOTE","CTA"] — typy byly v promptu povolené, ale LLM je do plánu nezařadil.
- `history_decisions` a `frequency_decisions` jsou prázdné → žádný downgrade kvůli historii v tomto běhu.

#### Mohla být scéna IMAGE?
- **Ano, a byla použita.** Narativ je čistě situační (telefon, obličej, laptop) — IMAGE sedí k observation/reveal režimu bez citátů nebo čísel.

#### Mohla být scéna PHONE?
- **Možné v principu** (v allowed / prompt types), ale voiceover nepopisuje konkrétní UI produktu ani screenshot aplikace — spíš generický social feed. PHONE by vyžadoval beat „ukázka na displeji“ s eligible assetem; `asset_usage` je prázdné.

#### Mohla být scéna QUOTE?
- **Nepravděpodobné** — brief neobsahuje schválený citát ani proof id; narativ je parafráze pain pointu, ne přímá citace.

#### Mohla být scéna STATISTIC?
- **V analyzer allowed_scene_types chybí** — worker by typ nepřijal bez úpravy plánu.

#### Mohla být scéna CHECKLIST?
- **Možné** u závěrečného „co udělat“ beatu, ale model zvolil poslední IMAGE (kalendář/queue) místo checklist karty; `requested_checklist_count: 0`.

#### Mohla být scéna CTA?
- **Možné** — CTA je v allowed a v prompt types, ale `requested_cta_count: 0` a finální výzva je mluvená + poslední still, ne typed CTA renderer.

### Proč zůstala IMAGE

Generátor konzistentně poslal AI image_prompt scény; presentation pass je nekonvertoval na typed renderery (žádný downgrade z IMAGE na jiný typ — naopak žádný požadavek na jiný typ v scene listu).

---

## 11. GLOBAL SUMMARY

| Package | Voice | Visual Profile | Scene Types | Semantic Motion | Typed Scenes Used | Assets Used | AI Images | Render Time | Warnings | Downgrades | History Decisions | CTA |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | ---: | --- | ---: | ---: | ---: | --- |
| The beauty salon that found five unread visitor questions on Tuesday — and no way to reach any of them | shimmer | NATURAL | IMAGE, IMAGE, IMAGE, IMAGE, IMAGE | ano (5 beatů) | ne | ano | 5 | 289.9 s | 0 | 0 | 0 | Create your AI assistant — let your website answer while the salon is closed. |

### Co fungovalo dobře

- Kompletní kreativní balíčky: voiceover, script, subtitles, platformové copy (včetně X variant), 3/3 videí dokončeno.
- EDITORIAL visual profile je konzistentně v promptech i v job input.
- Semantic motion beat metadata uložena u každého videa; TTS tail validation + Whisper titulky.

### Co se nepoužilo vůbec

- Typed scene renderery (CHECKLIST, PHONE, QUOTE, STATISTIC, CTA) — 0 v render_spec.
- Projektové assets ve scénách (`asset_usage` prázdné).
- Moderation fallback / local branded fallback.
- Alternativní TTS hlas (vše `alloy`).

### Nové systémy skutečně využité

- Visual profile EDITORIAL + verze `visual-profile@1`.
- Presentation analyzer + presentation_generation metadata na job input.
- Explicit scene plan + semantic motion v1.
- OpenAI TTS instructions z tone of voice + tail validation.
- Phrase subtitles + Whisper alignment (dle `debug.subtitle_source`).

### Dostupné, ale model / plán nevyužil

- CHECKLIST a CTA v `prompt_presentation_types` / `allowed_scene_types`.
- PHONE/QUOTE/STATISTIC v prompt allowlistu (kde byl v briefu), bez výběru v `visual_scenes`.
- Deterministický nebo preferred voice z knowledge.presentation (není nastaveno).

### Návrhy na zlepšení

- Vynutit minimálně jednu typed scénu na balíček, když je allowlisted a funnel stage sedí (např. CTA na conversion).
- U PHONE beats vyžadovat asset nebo explicitní `asset_usage` z knowledge.
- Persistovat storyboard beats (role, transition, text) do `render_spec` pro creative audit bez rekonstrukce.
- Persistovat sanitizovaný/final image prompt pro forenzní creative review.

## Zdroje dat (read-only)

- `getReviewRunExport("4633f34f-afce-4197-8cf9-79dce5ae2b72")`
- Tabulky: `production_runs`, `content_packages`, `content_items`, `video_jobs`, `content_strategy_items`
